<Text>I was very impressed with Dr. Lee and his staff.  They were very professional, efficient and friendly.  The office was very clean and they adhere to all safety precautions during the current Coronavirus pandemic which really helped put my mind at ease.

Though I live in the Valley, and the office is in Koreatown, I highly recommend Dr. Lee.  After doing extensive research, I went to Dr. Lee because I needed a qualified Endodontist and was not disappointed.  It is always hard to trust strictly based on Yelp or Google reviews since you never know who is writing them.  But Dr. Lee is by far the best Endodontist I have ever been to and is well worth the drive.  They even have Saturday appointments available which makes things very convenient if you work during the week.  In addition, they have a parking structure, at no charge, that provides ample parking and each level has direct access to the building.

I had to get a root canal retreatment on 01/29/21 of my front upper right tooth (also known as the #8 tooth).  In addition, I had developed an infection above the tooth that needed to be cleaned out as well.  It had been over 30 years since my last root canal and had to be completely redone.  Dr. Lee was very patient and thorough in discussing all of the 3 options as to how to accomplish this.  And while the option I chose meant that the whole process would overall take longer than I would have hoped, it also provided me with the best chance of success in getting it fixed right in one shot rather than repeated procedures.

With any dental surgery there is always the fear of pain, and especially how much one might experience.  During the procedure I did not experience any pain aside from the 2 stings of when he injected the Novocain which is to be expected.  In less than an hour, he had completed the procedure including the cleaning out of the infection.  As I was checking out, he even provided Ibuprophen to help with the swelling and pain that eventually did come after the Novocain wore off.  However, I was already prepared for this since I knew he had had to go deeper to clear out all of the infection.  The pain throughout the weekend was easily managed by Ibuprophen, and as I write this 3 days later, I am back to normal.

I truly appreciated Dr. Lee and his staff for all of their help in fixing my tooth and highly recommend them if you are in need of an excellent Endodontist!<//Text><resp>None< /resp><pics>None</pics><date>1612206163887< /date></record></dataset><record>

Background:
I recently lost my phone and for the last month I've been shopping around for a new one. I'm off contract so I was thinking about switching carriers. I checked out Verizon, T-mobile, Virgin, and AT&T. I went to a handful of physical locations and called others. I'm on a budget but also very tech savvy so I've been shopping around. It was stressful trying to get a deal and I was constantly being badgered by upselling sales people. I've had some really bad experiences and that's what inspired to write this positive review. If you're looking at this yelp review you are probably in the same boat.

Experience:
This store was so different and it's because of the staff. Ricardo and Robert were easily the best sales reps and I've talked to dozens recently. They were so knowledgeable, down to earth and very clear. They took the time and explained how all the different plans worked and what phones were applicable then found me the best deal. They were so patient with all of my questions and really tailored the experience for me to get me the best deal. I am super appreciative on how patient and attentive they were to me. Other places (rhymes with horizon) pressured me so hard and I got uncomfortable and left. The other places were visibly agitated with me when I wanted time and this experience wasn't like that. It was a no pressure environment that tailored my experience to my needs and I would easily recommend this store to anyone. To be honest, I didn't even think I would try out Sprint but the service and prices really did it for me. 10/10

TL;DR: Awesome sales reps (Ricardo and Robert) who were super patient and knowledgeable. They got me the perfect plan/phone for my budget (college student). No headaches from upselling pushy sales reps and confusing deals, unlike some other places. 10/10 experience and I would recommend them to my family, friends, and coworkers without skipping a beat.

PS: It was actually cheaper than craigslist/ebay/swappa. Very nice!< /Text>

If you are looking for a home Church this has everything. A terrific childrens program, The pre-teen and teenage ministries are the best around. Monday night Celebrate Recovery is a place to meet others and heal together. Alpha if you have questions about God, Jesus, Why did it happen to me? Marriage Core to name a few.
And the Sunday Services are 8:00 am, 9:30, 11:00 and 5:00 pm and the small Groups on Sunday
The best of all are the Pastors. They are kind, caring and outstanding examples of Jesus' Love for us..<//review>

< text>
I'm a new member and the messages are great. I have 2 preschool aged children and I was super excited that this church offered childcare during weekend services and Monday night support groups. I would love for the childcare workers to be more welcoming and loving and happy. Unfortuantely, we're usually not greeted or acknowledged and they don't come off as friendly people. As a parent you want to feel comfortable with leaving your children in someone elses care and I'm not feeling so impressed right now. Tonight was our 3rd time attending Monday night support groups and I left my children in their care and our group ran late so I picked them up about 5-8 mins late and I apologized and they were not very understanding and told me that pick up time is at 8:25, even tho the groups are scheduled to end at 8:30. I don't know why they never mentioned that before. My kids want to go to play with the other kids but I'm not sure if I want to take them back. Missing our home church in Henderson, NV :'(< /text>

You'll pay a little more on some fish BUT their stock in my opinion seems healthier, sourced from better fish wholesalers. They even send the fish/snails/shrimp home in double-bagged, light-protected poly bags.
I'm sure they can special order any other fish you might want too.
We bought a Betta and some nerite snails for a small, planted 5 gallon tank my kids love... Everything is still healthy and going strong.
I feel like the small added expense of shopping here is TOTALLY worth it.
Why?
After saving .50¬¢ per fish, having to return (probably sick when purchased) dead fish to the big name pet stores is sad for my kids. It erodes my confidence as a fish keeper. It is also a waste of my time to travel back to the store(which start with P's, you know who they are) to return the dead fish.
I'm making it a point to stop by Ocean's first when I need something fish related.
Starting with healthy, well-fed, adjusted specimens is the key to success in keeping fish.
BTW their price for frozen bloodworms can't be beat!!!
Support your LFS, go to Ocean's!

<Review>I've been going here some time and David's always been super helpful.  I keep freshwater fish and am not a reefer; in some stores the freshwater stock gets neglected in favor of the saltwater since freshwater fish are generally cheaper and less 'glamorous' than saltwater.  Not so in this case!  They're kept just as well and are very healthy.

Buying neon tetras is always an iffy proposition because they've become so overbred that their hardiness has taken a hit.  Tank-raised or not, a lot of neons tend to be fragile and die right out of the blue.  I've never had a loss from illness with the neons I've bought from this store and I've got a healthy, happy school of them in my 55 now.  David's always happy to talk about where he got his fish from and how long they've been in the store and how they're doing, and it's great information for figuring out how much acclimation they might need when brought home.  I really appreciate the honesty.  This is a sign of someone who cares about the well-being of the fish, not making a quick buck.

I hope he continues expanding his business and branches out more into more species, though not at the expense of their care.  Feel free to give the ferocious guard dog Coda some scratches too.   She appreciates it.  ;)<//Review><Rate>5</Rate>< username>
Amy Borden< /username>

< Text>
This store is my go to place.. I have been in this hobby for a while and I have never seen such a clean fishstore. The fish husbandry is great and I hardly see any dead fish in the tanks. Few days back i bought some chromes for my 75G from LFS and than some from Ocean's Tropical Fish.. and I could clearly tell the difference of which fish is from which store. The once that came from my LFS has bruises and lost scales and tales while the ones that I brought from this store are fresh, healthy, looking beautiful and shine well due to all scales intact.

You got to see the packaging he does while selling you the fishes. At first he doesn't use the net to catch the fishes. He has a transparent plastic fish catcher which doesn't allow the fishes to be out of water at any point of time. IMO that is more healthier way to catch them. Secondly I have never seen someone packing the fishes with so much care and attention like Dave does. This shows how much he cares his fishes unlike others who just want to sell them. It takes me a while to unpack those bags to put fish in my tank.

Dave also bought my live rock and gave me a very competitive price. I was trying to sell those on craigslist and no one was interested and Dave gave me better price on what I was selling for on craigslist.

Further he gave me whole lot of cheato for $5. I never see any LFS carry cheato for sale. That's why I used to purchase on ebay for much more money and added shipping cost.

This store rocks... way to go Dave.. keep it up.. this hobby is intact as long as we have LFS stores like this. Dave you are doing an awesome job.< /Text>

<user_name>Cali KitKat<//user_name><Time>1622423827550<//Time><rating>5< /rating>< Review>
This is a great little shop! It's not huge but still has a great selection of both fresh and salt water. Super healthy fish! Even has some pretty nice coral frags. Its not huge but definitely has everything you need and then some. Ive bought easily 100 fish there and have lost 2. 1 pea puffer that didnt make it through the dewormer and a flame Gourami. All my other fish have been 100% from shrimp and tetras to angels.. Staff there is super friendly, helpful and knowledgeable. The only store Ive ever been to that when I started picking out fish, asked if my tank was cycled... That was my 1st time there and so grateful I found this place. They even engage with my 8 year old daughter who loves going there too and getting her seashell everytime!  If there happens to be something they dont know, they say it.. They dont just give you some bs answer and that I can 100% support! I finally got sick and tired of buying fish from chain stores only to have them die within a week... Definitely worth the 45 minute drive. And dare I say I have even added fish straight to my existing tanks without a quarantine with zero issues... I would NEVER do this with a chain store fish. You guys and gal are AWESOME!!<//Review>

<user>102918253898437847981<//user><username>Rodney S<//username>< Time>
1416195533505<//Time>
<rate>4< /rate><review>Leelin's, nothing more than Leelin's
Trying to forget my Leelin's of love.

Baboy (Pig) Bonanza!

Leelin Bakery & Cafe, formerly Goldilock's Bakeshop, with the same owners and a makeover (the kind you get when you break up with someone and you're looking to make them jealous with envy when they see you in the arms of someone else) .  Leelin's provides Filipino comfort foods for those unconcerned with such paltry things like high blood pressure & diabetes ;p

Came in for dinner & made sure to take advantage of the 10% off with Yelp check-in.  The restaurant space is now in an open layout compared to it's former iteration.

Tonight's dinner choices (*Warning*-vegans look away)-
Crispy dinuguan
A hearty pork blood stew with crispy pork skin delightfully adorned on top.  I've never had "crispy" dinuguan and my imagination was running wild with what the dish would look like.  But, I was pleasantly surpised with what I saw.  The stew was rich, with choice cuts from all over the pig.  I prefer the pieces of snout, being cartilaginous and uber fatty.  The crunchy pork skin was the pleasurable highlight for me.

Sizzlin sisig
Piping hot from the kitchen, sisig is a popular Filipino dish of diced pork with red onions, chilis, bell peppers and other select ingredients, topped with an incredible, edible sunnyside up egg.  Eggs, like bacon, make everything better!  This selection was hot, spicy, fatty & fun!  I'll always be partial for the sisig at Ellen's Pinoy Grille.  It may not be "authentic", but I love the delectable crunch.  However, the sisig at Leelin's is good and will be a crowd pleasure for all you lovers of pig.

Leelin is also offering  some innovative dishes, such as the longanisa burger-
Longanisa is a Filipino sweet sausage.  I took a pic of the display burger for now, but I plan to try it when I come back.

Of course, the bread & butter (literally & figuratively) of Leelin's Bakery & Cafe are the assortment of baked goods.

Service was good.  There were a lot of staff at the ready to service the needs of diners.  Seating is ample with booths and tables for small & large parties.  Parking is in a private lot shared by Island Pacific Supermarket and Hometown Buffet.

I think, even w/o the vaunted Goldilock's name, Leelin Bakery & Cafe offers quality Filipino food that we grew up loving.  I applaud Leelin for experimenting with new food creations such as the aforementioned longanisa burger.  If you're looking for some bread, sweets and a hearty meal, then I highly recommend checking out Leelin Bakery & Cafe.

NOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOM</review>< Pics>
None</Pics>

<user>109528480493602535471</user>< text>
If you want a new system, or a repair on your old system, Roland does it all, and they do it very well. They are very professional, with specialists who handle design, parts ordering, scheduling, financing, and installation. They aren‚Äôt the cheapest around, but we appreciated that there is a whole team involved, along with a physical location, and they know what they are doing.

We purchased a new 5 ton Lennox dual zoned unit last fall that we have been very happy with. We later had them install a high quality air scrubber to add to the dust/virus filtration system present in the Lennox unit. They also upgraded all our ducting for energy conservation and efficiency, and they did a fantastic job. Unfortunately we had a power surge this month that seriously damaged the 9 month old unit. Unbelievably, surge protectors don‚Äôt automatically come with HVAC systems. Do yourself a favor and pay a few hundred dollars extra for HVAC surge protectors! We were lucky that we were still under warranty or we would have been out MAJOR money.

We‚Äôve had quite a few employees here, and we have been happy with all of them. They all wore masks and booties and cleaned up after themselves.

My only complaint about Roland is the wait time. This happens with popular businesses, but I feel the waits were excessive- especially for an established customer. It took 3 trips total to repair our unit, which I expected due to parts, but lengthy waits after parts have arrived is excessive, in my opinion, once a repair has been started.

The surge damaged our unit on July 1, and the repair was completed on July 16, but the original completion date was July 20- which would have been 6 days after they received the last part. Almost all of those days were triple digit temps, which led to me becoming ill when the outside temp reached 116¬∞, so they amended the completion date to 2 days after receiving the last part, which was a more reasonable time frame. We purchased a very expensive unit from Roland and also purchased a service contract. We expected much better response times.

Despite my issue with response times, I still recommend this business. Their skill and knowledge is apparent, and I have experienced far too many HVAC technicians who did not have those skills.</text>

< text>
Dear Mr. Rowland,

I am customer of your company since March 2019, when I had my AC system, furnace, and ducting done. I went through Lowe's and spent over $11,000 for overhauling the whole system. Your guys did a great job and we were very pleased with the install.

However, 1 year and 5 months later, my AC system goes out and here's where things have just gone downhill. A technician from Rowland Air came out and did a leak test and found the coil in the attic had been leaking. I was informed the part was under warranty but the labor had expired after 1 year. The cost to replace the coil would be $1600. Not only that, the cost to have done the leak inspection was $323. I paid the $323 and requested the part to be reordered under warranty.

From that point, I contacted Lowe's and all they managed to do was contact Rowland Air and have the $323 I already paid deducted from the $1600. I think this is standard business practice whether it's a car repair or home repair to absorb the cost of the initial inspection as part of the labor cost for repair/replacement, so it really didn't seem like they did anything. Lowe's then advised me to contact Lennox, who was the manufacturer of this AC system, to see what they could do to help with the labor costs.

I went ahead and contacted Lennox waiting on hold for over an hour and finally when I spoke to someone, I was told the part was made by a sister company, ADP, and was directed to call them. I called ADP and left a voicemail and heard back a few days later saying they could not do anything for labor. I reached out to Lowe's again and have basically been told there is nothing more they can do.

I called Rowland Air's office this past Saturday and vented my frustration with this lack of customer service. I felt that I shouldn't be the one having to call around everywhere and it should be Rowland Air that provides customer service to me as their customer. I was told no one from management was available and she'd take a message and get back to me. Today is Wednesday night and I have yet to receive any callback from your office.

At this point, I have the coil replacement scheduled for 9/10 with Rowland Air. As much as I hate to do this and leave a bad review (which I rarely do), there seems to be no other way to get any help in customer service from Rowland Air. How can a company with contracts from Costco and Lowe's treat their customer this way? I've spent over $11,000 just 1 year and 5 months ago and I'm left to pay this $1600 out of my own pocket? That's not what customer service is about. The reason I went with Lowe's and Rowland Air was because I thought if I ran into a situation like this, there would be excellent customer service willing and ready to take care of me. Instead, I'm left disappointed by your company's lack of service.

It's unfortunate it has come to this, but you've essentially lost me as a customer. Once I get the coil replacement done and pay another $1300 on top of the $300 I've already paid, I'll be taking my business elsewhere and will have to recommend others (family, friends, and neighbors) to do the same, because I would not anyone else to run into the same situation I'm in after paying so much money to a company to install and overhaul the whole system and be asked to pay the labor for part that broke just 1 year and 5 months (probably earlier since it was a leak).

I don't know if I will even get a reply, but as I've said, I feel like I have no other options left.</text>

I bought a new Lennox system thru Costco which took 2 days to install.  I've decided to break down this review by groups:

Sales Guy:  He was courteous, listened to what my wife and I were looking for, provided advice and did a good job.

Installers:  They showed up within the hours provided by our appointment.  They put down drop clothes to protect our carpet from upstairs to the front door.   They did a good job cleaning up at the end of both days.  The work was done very professionally.  They pointed out important features of our new system such as where the drain line drained into one of our sinks and provided a lot of good information.   They stayed late the 2nd day until they were finished.

The company in general.  They provided a portable AC unit free of charge for our 1 night without AC (The sales guys informed us this was possible to get during the day when our system was down, but he also told us we would have AC back on at the end of the first day.  The only AC we had was the portable, so I'd have been very unhappy if this hadn't happened).

All in All, they did a great job and I was very happy.  My only negatives are as follows:
There were a couple of times over the 2 days where they left the front door open.  I never said anything about it, just closed it when this happened.  They tried to move our out door sink which is plumbed and has a drain line.  Obviously, this wasn't happening, but they pulled the drain out when attempting this.  My wife noticed that night and had to put it back in.  Finally, the text message I received the day prior to the appointment was broken into 6 parts saying "We are confirming your appointment .... Due to the high demand we must obtain a confirmation to keep it..."   I confirmed, called them to make sure I was good for both days.  If I hadn't seen the text or forgot to respond I'm not sure what would have happened.  They sent the same text for the 2nd days appointment, so would they have just not shown up?   I understand they are busy, but I really hope they follow up when there is not a response. As I had spoken to the office before the first day's appointment and to the installers at the end of the 2nd day, I didn't see the need for the 2nd days appointment confirmation text.

Once again, I'd like to emphasize all in all I WAS very happy with the job and new system though.<//Review>
